    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 12pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Glenville, New York &#8211;</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">&#160;</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">January 10, 2025</font></div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">TrustCo Bank Corp NY <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">(TrustCo, Nasdaq: TRST)</font> today announced that it will release fourth quarter
      2024 results after the market close on January 21, 2025.&#160; Results are released on the 21<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">st</sup> of the reporting months (January, April, July and October), or on the next day that equity markets are open if the 21<sup style="vertical-align: text-top; line-height: 1; font-size: smaller;">st</sup> falls on a
      Friday, weekend or holiday.&#160; A conference call to discuss the results will be held at 9:00 a.m. Eastern Time on January 22, 2025.&#160; Those wishing to participate in the call may dial toll-free <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">for the United States at 1-833-470-1428, and for Canada at 1-833-950-0062, </font>Access code 645488.<font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">&#160; </font>A replay of the call will be available for thirty days by
      dialing <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">toll-free for the United States at 1-866-813-9403, </font>Access code 619481.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #000000;">The call will also be audio webcast at</font><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #3C4043;">&#160;</font><u><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">https://events.q4i<font style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">nc.com/attendee/773359679</font></font></u><font style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: #000000;">, </font><font style="font-size: 10pt;"><font style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">and will be available for one year.&#160; The earnings press release will be posted on the Company&#8217;s Investor Relations website at: <font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';"><u>https://trustcobank.q4ir.com/corporate-overview/corporate-profile/default.aspx.</u></font></font><font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);"><font style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">&#160;</font>
          Other information, including the Company&#8217;s most recent annual report, proxy statement and filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission can also be found at this website.</font></font></div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>

      Jersey, Vermont, Massachusetts, and Florida.&#160; For more information, visit www.trustcobank.com.</div>
